It looks like a German history book.

Scales and whatever else, I don't really get it.

"The Story of a Certain Man - Chapter 1"

Uh, the title is... oops, I can't get absorbed in reading in a place like this, I'll save it for another time.

It looks like an architecture book.

That would definitely be confusing...
The word for "floor" is "floor" in English, and apparently "Stock" in German.
It looks like an architectural science book.
I flip through a book that caught my eye.
It looks like a commentary on maps.

So only East changes... well, I guess everything besides the first letter is different though.
